import 'package:flutter/services.dart';

class PopScopeWrapper extends StatefulWidget {
const PopScopeWrapper({
super.key,
this.width,
this.height,
required this.onBack,
});

final double? width;
final double? height;
final Future Function() onBack;

@override
State<PopScopeWrapper> createState() => _PopScopeWrapperState();
}

class _PopScopeWrapperState extends State<PopScopeWrapper> {
@override
Widget build(BuildContext context) {
return WillPopScope(
onWillPop: () async {
await widget.onBack();

return false; // –ë–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä—É–µ–º —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω—ã–π pop
},
child: SizedBox(
width: widget.width ?? double.infinity,
height: widget.height ?? double.infinity,
),
);
}
}

final QrBarCodeScannerDialog _scanner = QrBarCodeScannerDialog();

Future<String?> scanBarcodeAndReturn(
BuildContext context,
String? title,
) async {
try {
Completer<String?> completer = Completer<String?>();

_scanner.getScannedQrBarCode(
context: context,
cameraFacing: CameraFacing.back,
onCode: (rawCode) {
if (rawCode != null && rawCode.trim().isNotEmpty) {
// –£–¥–∞–ª—è–µ–º –ø—Ä–µ—Ñ–∏–∫—Å "Code scanned = " –µ—Å–ª–∏ –æ–Ω –µ—Å—Ç—å

rawCode.replaceFirst(RegExp(r'^Code scanned =\s*'), '').trim();
completer.complete(cleaned);
} else {
completer.complete(null);
}
},
);

} catch (e) {

import 'dart:convert';
String? convertBytesToBase64(FFUploadedFile? bytes) {
  /// MODIFY CODE ONLY BELOW THIS LINE
  if (bytes == null) return null;
  final fileBytes = bytes.bytes;
  if (fileBytes == null || fileBytes.isEmpty) return null;
  return base64Encode(fileBytes);
  /// MODIFY CODE ONLY ABOVE THIS LINE
}

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION delete_old_records()
RETURNS void AS $$
BEGIN
  DELETE FROM your_table_name
  WHERE id NOT IN (
    SELECT id
    FROM (
      SELECT id
      FROM your_table_name
      ORDER BY created_at DESC
      LIMIT 2
    ) AS last_two
  );
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;
